class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Method</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Function</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Constructor</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Field</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Variable</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Class</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Interface</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Module</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Property</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Unit</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Value</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Enum</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Keyword</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Snippet</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Color</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Reference</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.File</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Folder</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.EnumMember</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Constant</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Struct</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Event</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Operator</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.TypeParameter</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The <a href="#CompletionItemKind">kind</a> of the completion.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#CompletionItem" class="type-ref">CompletionItem</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

#### Properties

<span id="CompletionItem.additionalTextEdits"></span><span id="807" class="ts" data-target="#details-807" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">additionalTextEdits</span>?: <a href="#TextEdit" class="type-ref">TextEdit</a>\[\]</span>

An optional array of additional [text edits](#TextEdit) that are applied when selecting this completion. Edits must not overlap with the main [edit](#CompletionItem.textEdit) nor with themselves.

<span id="CompletionItem.command"></span><span id="808" class="ts" data-target="#details-808" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">command</span>?: <a href="#Command" class="type-ref">Command</a></span>

An optional [command](#Command) that is executed _after_ inserting this completion. _Note_ that additional modifications to the current document should be described with the [additionalTextEdits](#CompletionItem.additionalTextEdits)-property.

<span id="CompletionItem.commitCharacters"></span><span id="805" class="ts" data-target="#details-805" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">commitCharacters</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>\[\]</span>

An optional set of characters that when pressed while this completion is active will accept it first and then type that character. _Note_ that all commit characters should have `length=1` and that superfluous characters will be ignored.

<span id="CompletionItem.detail"></span><span id="799" class="ts" data-target="#details-799" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">detail</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A human-readable string with additional information about this item, like type or symbol information.

<span id="CompletionItem.documentation"></span><span id="800" class="ts" data-target="#details-800" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">documentation</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A human-readable string that represents a doc-comment.

<span id="CompletionItem.filterText"></span><span id="802" class="ts" data-target="#details-802" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">filterText</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A string that should be used when filtering a set of completion items. When `falsy` the [label](#CompletionItem.label) is used.

<span id="CompletionItem.insertText"></span><span id="803" class="ts" data-target="#details-803" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">insertText</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span>

A string or snippet that should be inserted in a document when selecting this completion. When `falsy` the [label](#CompletionItem.label) is used.

<span id="CompletionItem.kind"></span><span id="798" class="ts" data-target="#details-798" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">kind</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Text</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Method</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Function</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Constructor</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Field</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Variable</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Class</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Interface</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Module</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Property</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Unit</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Value</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Enum</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Keyword</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Snippet</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Color</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Reference</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.File</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Folder</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.EnumMember</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Constant</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Struct</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Event</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.Operator</span> | <span class="type-unknown">CompletionItemKind.TypeParameter</span></span>

The kind of this completion item. Based on the kind an icon is chosen by the editor.

<span id="CompletionItem.label"></span><span id="797" class="ts" data-target="#details-797" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">label</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The label of this completion item. By default this is also the text that is inserted when selecting this completion.

<span id="CompletionItem.range"></span><span id="804" class="ts" data-target="#details-804" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span>?: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

A range of text that should be replaced by this completion item.

Defaults to a range from the start of the [current word](#TextDocument.getWordRangeAtPosition) to the current position.

_Note:_ The range must be a [single line](#Range.isSingleLine) and it must [contain](#Range.contains) the position at which completion has been [requested](#CompletionItemProvider.provideCompletionItems).

<span id="CompletionItem.sortText"></span><span id="801" class="ts" data-target="#details-801" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">sortText</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A string that should be used when comparing this item with other items. When `falsy` the [label](#CompletionItem.label) is used.

<span id="CompletionItem.textEdit"></span><span id="806" class="ts" data-target="#details-806" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">textEdit</span>?: <a href="#TextEdit" class="type-ref">TextEdit</a></span>

- _deprecated_ - Use `CompletionItem.insertText` and `CompletionItem.range` instead.

<s>An [edit](#TextEdit) which is applied to a document when selecting this completion. When an edit is provided the value of [insertText](#CompletionItem.insertText) is ignored.</s>

<s>The [range](#Range) of the edit must be single-line and on the same line completions were [requested](#CompletionItemProvider.provideCompletionItems) at.</s>

### <span id="CompletionItemProvider"></span><span id="820" class="code-item">CompletionItemProvider</span>

The completion item provider interface defines the contract between extensions and [IntelliSense](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/intellisense).

When computing _complete_ completion items is expensive, providers can optionally implement the `resolveCompletionItem`-function. In that case it is enough to return completion items with a [label](#CompletionItem.label) from the [provideCompletionItems](#CompletionItemProvider.provideCompletionItems)-function. Subsequently, when a completion item is shown in the UI and gains focus this provider is asked to resolve the item, like adding [doc-comment](#CompletionItem.documentation) or [details](#CompletionItem.detail).

Providers are asked for completions either explicitly by a user gesture or -depending on the configuration- implicitly when typing words or trigger characters.

#### Methods

<span id="CompletionItemProvider.provideCompletionItems"></span><span id="822" class="ts" data-target="#details-822" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideCompletionItems</span>(<span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a>, <span class="ident">position</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#CompletionItem" class="type-ref">CompletionItem</a>\[\] | <a href="#CompletionList" class="type-ref">CompletionList</a>&gt;</span>

Provide completion items for the given position and document.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="document"></span><span id="823" class="ts" data-target="#details-823" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">document</span><span>: </span><a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The document in which the command was invoked.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="position"></span><span id="824" class="ts" data-target="#details-824" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">position</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The position at which the command was invoked.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="825" class="ts" data-target="#details-825" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#CompletionItem" class="type-ref">CompletionItem</a>[] | <a href="#CompletionList" class="type-ref">CompletionList</a>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>An array of completions, a <a href="#CompletionList">completion list</a>, or a thenable that resolves to either. The lack of a result can be signaled by returning <code>undefined</code>, <code>null</code>, or an empty array.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="CompletionItemProvider.resolveCompletionItem"></span><span id="827" class="ts" data-target="#details-827" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">resolveCompletionItem</span>(<span class="ident">item</span>: <a href="#CompletionItem" class="type-ref">CompletionItem</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#CompletionItem" class="type-ref">CompletionItem</a>&gt;</span>

Given a completion item fill in more data, like [doc-comment](#CompletionItem.documentation) or [details](#CompletionItem.detail).

The editor will only resolve a completion item once.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="item"></span><span id="828" class="ts" data-target="#details-828" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">item</span><span>: </span><a href="#CompletionItem" class="type-ref">CompletionItem</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A completion item currently active in the UI.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="829" class="ts" data-target="#details-829" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#CompletionItem" class="type-ref">CompletionItem</a>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The resolved completion item or a thenable that resolves to of such. It is OK to return the given <code>item</code>. When no result is returned, the given <code>item</code> will be used.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="DecorationRenderOptions"></span><span id="280" class="code-item">DecorationRenderOptions</span>

Represents rendering styles for a [text editor decoration](#TextEditorDecorationType).

#### Properties

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.after"></span><span id="305" class="ts" data-target="#details-305" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">after</span>?: <a href="#ThemableDecorationAttachmentRenderOptions" class="type-ref">ThemableDecorationAttachmentRenderOptions</a></span>

Defines the rendering options of the attachment that is inserted after the decorated text

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.backgroundColor"></span><span id="286" class="ts" data-target="#details-286" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">backgroundColor</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a></span>

Background color of the decoration. Use rgba() and define transparent background colors to play well with other decorations. Alternativly a color from the color registry an be [referenced](#ColorIdentifier).

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.before"></span><span id="304" class="ts" data-target="#details-304" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">before</span>?: <a href="#ThemableDecorationAttachmentRenderOptions" class="type-ref">ThemableDecorationAttachmentRenderOptions</a></span>

Defines the rendering options of the attachment that is inserted before the decorated text

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.border"></span><span id="291" class="ts" data-target="#details-291" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">border</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.borderColor"></span><span id="292" class="ts" data-target="#details-292" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">borderColor</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'border' for setting one or more of the individual border properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.borderRadius"></span><span id="293" class="ts" data-target="#details-293" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">borderRadius</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'border' for setting one or more of the individual border properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.borderSpacing"></span><span id="294" class="ts" data-target="#details-294" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">borderSpacing</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'border' for setting one or more of the individual border properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.borderStyle"></span><span id="295" class="ts" data-target="#details-295" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">borderStyle</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'border' for setting one or more of the individual border properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.borderWidth"></span><span id="296" class="ts" data-target="#details-296" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">borderWidth</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'border' for setting one or more of the individual border properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.color"></span><span id="299" class="ts" data-target="#details-299" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">color</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.cursor"></span><span id="298" class="ts" data-target="#details-298" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">cursor</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.dark"></span><span id="285" class="ts" data-target="#details-285" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">dark</span>?: <a href="#ThemableDecorationRenderOptions" class="type-ref">ThemableDecorationRenderOptions</a></span>

Overwrite options for dark themes.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.gutterIconPath"></span><span id="301" class="ts" data-target="#details-301" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">gutterIconPath</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span>

An **absolute path** or an URI to an image to be rendered in the gutter.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.gutterIconSize"></span><span id="302" class="ts" data-target="#details-302" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">gutterIconSize</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Specifies the size of the gutter icon. Available values are 'auto', 'contain', 'cover' and any percentage value. For further information: <https://msdn.microsoft.com/en-us/library/jj127316(v=vs.85).aspx>

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.isWholeLine"></span><span id="281" class="ts" data-target="#details-281" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isWholeLine</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Should the decoration be rendered also on the whitespace after the line text. Defaults to `false`.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.letterSpacing"></span><span id="300" class="ts" data-target="#details-300" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">letterSpacing</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.light"></span><span id="284" class="ts" data-target="#details-284" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">light</span>?: <a href="#ThemableDecorationRenderOptions" class="type-ref">ThemableDecorationRenderOptions</a></span>

Overwrite options for light themes.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.outline"></span><span id="287" class="ts" data-target="#details-287" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">outline</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.outlineColor"></span><span id="288" class="ts" data-target="#details-288" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">outlineColor</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'outline' for setting one or more of the individual outline properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.outlineStyle"></span><span id="289" class="ts" data-target="#details-289" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">outlineStyle</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'outline' for setting one or more of the individual outline properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.outlineWidth"></span><span id="290" class="ts" data-target="#details-290" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">outlineWidth</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration. Better use 'outline' for setting one or more of the individual outline properties.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.overviewRulerColor"></span><span id="303" class="ts" data-target="#details-303" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">overviewRulerColor</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a></span>

The color of the decoration in the overview ruler. Use rgba() and define transparent colors to play well with other decorations.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.overviewRulerLane"></span><span id="283" class="ts" data-target="#details-283" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">overviewRulerLane</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">OverviewRulerLane.Left</span> | <span class="type-unknown">OverviewRulerLane.Center</span> | <span class="type-unknown">OverviewRulerLane.Right</span> | <span class="type-unknown">OverviewRulerLane.Full</span></span>

The position in the overview ruler where the decoration should be rendered.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.rangeBehavior"></span><span id="282" class="ts" data-target="#details-282" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">rangeBehavior</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">DecorationRangeBehavior.OpenOpen</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DecorationRangeBehavior.ClosedClosed</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DecorationRangeBehavior.OpenClosed</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DecorationRangeBehavior.ClosedOpen</span></span>

Customize the growing behavior of the decoration when edits occur at the edges of the decoration's range. Defaults to `DecorationRangeBehavior.OpenOpen`.

<span id="DecorationRenderOptions.textDecoration"></span><span id="297" class="ts" data-target="#details-297" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">textDecoration</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

CSS styling property that will be applied to text enclosed by a decoration.

### <span id="Definition"></span><span id="1274" class="code-item">Definition</span>

The definition of a symbol represented as one or many [locations](#Location). For most programming languages there is only one location at which a symbol is defined.

<span id="Definition"></span><span id="1274" class="ts" data-target="#details-1274" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">Definition</span>: <a href="#Location" class="type-ref">Location</a> | <a href="#Location" class="type-ref">Location</a>\[\]</span>

### <span id="DefinitionProvider"></span><span id="522" class="code-item">DefinitionProvider</span>

The definition provider interface defines the contract between extensions and the [go to definition](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/editingevolved#_go-to-definition) and peek definition features.

#### Methods

<span id="DefinitionProvider.provideDefinition"></span><span id="524" class="ts" data-target="#details-524" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideDefinition</span>(<span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a>, <span class="ident">position</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Definition" class="type-ref">Definition</a>&gt;</span>

Provide the definition of the symbol at the given position and document.

### <span id="Diagnostic"></span><span id="934" class="code-item">Diagnostic</span>

Represents a diagnostic, such as a compiler error or warning. Diagnostic objects are only valid in the scope of a file.

#### Constructors

<span id="Diagnostic.new Diagnostic"></span><span id="941" class="ts" data-target="#details-941" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Diagnostic</span>(<span class="ident">range</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>, <span class="ident">message</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">severity</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Error</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Warning</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Information</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Hint</span>): <a href="#Diagnostic" class="type-ref">Diagnostic</a></span>

Creates a new diagnostic object.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="range"></span><span id="942" class="ts" data-target="#details-942" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The range to which this diagnostic applies.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="message"></span><span id="943" class="ts" data-target="#details-943" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">message</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The human-readable message.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="severity"></span><span id="944" class="ts" data-target="#details-944" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">severity</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Error</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Warning</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Information</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Hint</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The severity, default is <a href="#DiagnosticSeverity.Error">error</a>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Diagnostic" class="type-ref">Diagnostic</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

#### Properties

<span id="Diagnostic.code"></span><span id="939" class="ts" data-target="#details-939" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">code</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

A code or identifier for this diagnostics. Will not be surfaced to the user, but should be used for later processing, e.g. when providing [code actions](#CodeActionContext).

<span id="Diagnostic.message"></span><span id="936" class="ts" data-target="#details-936" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">message</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The human-readable message.

<span id="Diagnostic.range"></span><span id="935" class="ts" data-target="#details-935" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

The range to which this diagnostic applies.

<span id="Diagnostic.severity"></span><span id="938" class="ts" data-target="#details-938" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">severity</span>: <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Error</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Warning</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Information</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DiagnosticSeverity.Hint</span></span>

The severity, default is [error](#DiagnosticSeverity.Error).

<span id="Diagnostic.source"></span><span id="937" class="ts" data-target="#details-937" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">source</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A human-readable string describing the source of this diagnostic, e.g. 'typescript' or 'super lint'.

### <span id="DiagnosticCollection"></span><span id="945" class="code-item">DiagnosticCollection</span>

A diagnostics collection is a container that manages a set of [diagnostics](#Diagnostic). Diagnostics are always scopes to a diagnostics collection and a resource.

To get an instance of a `DiagnosticCollection` use [createDiagnosticCollection](#languages.createDiagnosticCollection).

#### Properties

<span id="DiagnosticCollection.name"></span><span id="946" class="ts" data-target="#details-946" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">name</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The name of this diagnostic collection, for instance `typescript`. Every diagnostic from this collection will be associated with this name. Also, the task framework uses this name when defining [problem matchers](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/tasks#_defining-a-problem-matcher).

#### Methods

<span id="DiagnosticCollection.clear"></span><span id="957" class="ts" data-target="#details-957" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">clear</span>(): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Remove all diagnostics from this collection. The same as calling `#set(undefined)`;

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><td><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></td><td><div class="comment"></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="DiagnosticCollection.delete"></span><span id="954" class="ts" data-target="#details-954" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">delete</span>(<span class="ident">uri</span>: <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Remove all diagnostics from this collection that belong to the provided `uri`. The same as `#set(uri, undefined)`.

<span id="DiagnosticCollection.set"></span><span id="948" class="ts" data-target="#details-948" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">set</span>(<span class="ident">uri</span>: <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>, <span class="ident">diagnostics</span>: <a href="#Diagnostic" class="type-ref">Diagnostic</a>\[\] | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="uri"></span><span id="949" class="ts" data-target="#details-949" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">uri</span><span>: </span><a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A resource identifier.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="diagnostics"></span><span id="950" class="ts" data-target="#details-950" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">diagnostics</span><span>: </span><a href="#Diagnostic" class="type-ref">Diagnostic</a>[] | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Array of diagnostics or <code>undefined</code></p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="DiagnosticCollection.set"></span><span id="951" class="ts" data-target="#details-951" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">set</span>(<span class="ident">entries</span>: \[<a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>, <a href="#Diagnostic" class="type-ref">Diagnostic</a>\[\] | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span>\]\[\]): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Replace all entries in this collection.

Diagnostics of multiple tuples of the same uri will be merged, e.g `[[file1, [d1]], [file1, [d2]]]` is equivalent to `[[file1, [d1, d2]]]`. If a diagnostics item is `undefined` as in `[file1, undefined]` all previous but not subsequent diagnostics are removed.

### <span id="DiagnosticSeverity"></span><span id="929" class="code-item">DiagnosticSeverity</span>

Represents the severity of diagnostics.

#### Enumeration members

<span id="DiagnosticSeverity.Error"></span><span id="930" class="ts" data-target="#details-930" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">Error</span></span>

_0_

<span id="DiagnosticSeverity.Hint"></span><span id="933" class="ts" data-target="#details-933" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">Hint</span></span>

_3_

<span id="DiagnosticSeverity.Information"></span><span id="932" class="ts" data-target="#details-932" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">Information</span></span>

_2_

### <span id="Disposable"></span><span id="409" class="code-item">Disposable</span>

Represents a type which can release resources, such as event listening or a timer.

#### Static

<span id="Disposable.from"></span><span id="411" class="ts" data-target="#details-411" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">from</span>(...<span class="ident">disposableLikes</span>: {dispose: () => <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>}\[\]): <a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a></span>

Combine many disposable-likes into one. Use this method when having objects with a dispose function which are not instances of Disposable.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="disposableLikes"></span><span id="412" class="ts" data-target="#details-412" data-toggle="collapse"><span>...</span><span class="ident">disposableLikes</span><span>: </span>{dispose: () =&gt; <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>}[]</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Objects that have at least a <code>dispose</code>-function member.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Returns a new disposable which, upon dispose, will dispose all provided disposables.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

#### Constructors

<span id="Disposable.new Disposable"></span><span id="418" class="ts" data-target="#details-418" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Disposable</span>(<span class="ident">callOnDispose</span>: <a href="#Function" class="type-ref">Function</a>): <a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a></span>

Creates a new Disposable calling the provided function on dispose.

### <span id="DocumentFilter"></span><span id="491" class="code-item">DocumentFilter</span>

A document filter denotes a document by different properties like the [language](#TextDocument.languageId), the [scheme](#Uri.scheme) of its resource, or a glob-pattern that is applied to the [path](#TextDocument.fileName).

- _sample_ - A language filter that applies to typescript files on disk: `{ language: 'typescript', scheme: 'file' }`

<!-- -->

- _sample_ - A language filter that applies to all package.json paths: `{ language: 'json', pattern: '**∕package.json' }`

#### Properties

<span id="DocumentFilter.language"></span><span id="492" class="ts" data-target="#details-492" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">language</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A language id, like `typescript`.

<span id="DocumentFilter.pattern"></span><span id="494" class="ts" data-target="#details-494" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">pattern</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A glob pattern, like `*.{ts,js}`.

<span id="DocumentFilter.scheme"></span><span id="493" class="ts" data-target="#details-493" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">scheme</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A Uri [scheme](#Uri.scheme), like `file` or `untitled`.

Provide formatting edits for a whole document.

### <span id="DocumentHighlight"></span><span id="557" class="code-item">DocumentHighlight</span>

A document highlight is a range inside a text document which deserves special attention. Usually a document highlight is visualized by changing the background color of its range.

#### Constructors

<span id="DocumentHighlight.new DocumentHighlight"></span><span id="561" class="ts" data-target="#details-561" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new DocumentHighlight</span>(<span class="ident">range</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>, <span class="ident">kind</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">DocumentHighlightKind.Text</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DocumentHighlightKind.Read</span> | <span class="type-unknown">DocumentHighlightKind.Write</span>): <a href="#DocumentHighlight" class="type-ref">DocumentHighlight</a></span>

Creates a new document highlight object.

### <span id="DocumentLinkProvider"></span><span id="837" class="code-item">DocumentLinkProvider</span>

The document link provider defines the contract between extensions and feature of showing links in the editor.

#### Methods

<span id="DocumentLinkProvider.provideDocumentLinks"></span><span id="839" class="ts" data-target="#details-839" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideDocumentLinks</span>(<span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#DocumentLink" class="type-ref">DocumentLink</a>\[\]&gt;</span>

Provide links for the given document. Note that the editor ships with a default provider that detects `http(s)` and `file` links.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="document"></span><span id="840" class="ts" data-target="#details-840" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">document</span><span>: </span><a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The document in which the command was invoked.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="841" class="ts" data-target="#details-841" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#DocumentLink" class="type-ref">DocumentLink</a>[]&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>An array of <a href="#DocumentLink">document links</a> or a thenable that resolves to such. The lack of a result can be signaled by returning <code>undefined</code>, <code>null</code>, or an empty array.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="DocumentLinkProvider.resolveDocumentLink"></span><span id="843" class="ts" data-target="#details-843" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">resolveDocumentLink</span>(<span class="ident">link</span>: <a href="#DocumentLink" class="type-ref">DocumentLink</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#DocumentLink" class="type-ref">DocumentLink</a>&gt;</span>

Given a link fill in its [target](#DocumentLink.target). This method is called when an incomplete link is selected in the UI. Providers can implement this method and return incomple links (without target) from the [`provideDocumentLinks`](#DocumentLinkProvider.provideDocumentLinks) method which often helps to improve performance.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="link"></span><span id="844" class="ts" data-target="#details-844" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">link</span><span>: </span><a href="#DocumentLink" class="type-ref">DocumentLink</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The link that is to be resolved.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="845" class="ts" data-target="#details-845" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#DocumentLink" class="type-ref">DocumentLink</a>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="DocumentRangeFormattingEditProvider"></span><span id="730" class="code-item">DocumentRangeFormattingEditProvider</span>

The document formatting provider interface defines the contract between extensions and the formatting-feature.

#### Methods

<span id="DocumentRangeFormattingEditProvider.provideDocumentRangeFormattingEdits"></span><span id="732" class="ts" data-target="#details-732" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideDocumentRangeFormattingEdits</span>(<span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a>, <span class="ident">range</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>, <span class="ident">options</span>: <a href="#FormattingOptions" class="type-ref">FormattingOptions</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#TextEdit" class="type-ref">TextEdit</a>\[\]&gt;</span>

Provide formatting edits for a range in a document.

The given range is a hint and providers can decide to format a smaller or larger range. Often this is done by adjusting the start and end of the range to full syntax nodes.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="document"></span><span id="733" class="ts" data-target="#details-733" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">document</span><span>: </span><a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The document in which the command was invoked.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="range"></span><span id="734" class="ts" data-target="#details-734" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The range which should be formatted.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="options"></span><span id="735" class="ts" data-target="#details-735" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">options</span><span>: </span><a href="#FormattingOptions" class="type-ref">FormattingOptions</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Options controlling formatting.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="736" class="ts" data-target="#details-736" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#TextEdit" class="type-ref">TextEdit</a>[]&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A set of text edits or a thenable that resolves to such. ### <span id="DocumentSelector"></span><span id="1272" class="code-item">DocumentSelector</span>

A language selector is the combination of one or many language identifiers and [language filters](#DocumentFilter).

- _sample_ - `let sel:DocumentSelector = 'typescript'`;

<!-- -->

- _sample_ - `let sel:DocumentSelector = ['typescript', { language: 'json', pattern: '**∕tsconfig.json' }]`;

<span id="DocumentSelector"></span><span id="1272" class="ts" data-target="#details-1272" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">DocumentSelector</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#DocumentFilter" class="type-ref">DocumentFilter</a> | <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#DocumentFilter" class="type-ref">DocumentFilter</a>\[\]</span>

### <span id="Event"></span><span id="422" class="code-item">Event&lt;T></span>

Represents a typed event.

A function that represents an event to which you subscribe by calling it with a listener function as argument.

- _sample_ - `item.onDidChange(function(event) { console.log("Event happened: " + event); });`

<span id="__call"></span><span id="424" class="ts" data-target="#details-424" toggle="collapse">(<span class="ident">listener</span>: (e: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>) => <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>, <span class="ident">thisArgs</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>, <span class="ident">disposables</span>?: <a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a>\[\]): <a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a></span>

A function that represents an event to which you subscribe by calling it with a listener function as argument.

A function that represents an event to which you subscribe by calling it with a listener function as argument.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="listener"></span><span id="425" class="ts" data-target="#details-425" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">listener</span><span>: </span>(e: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>) =&gt; <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The listener function will be called when the event happens.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="thisArgs"></span><span id="429" class="ts" data-target="#details-429" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">thisArgs</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">any</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The <code>this</code>-argument which will be used when calling the event listener.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="disposables"></span><span id="430" class="ts" data-target="#details-430" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">disposables</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a>[]</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>An array to which a <a href="#Disposable">disposable</a> will be added.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A disposable which unsubscribes the event listener.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="EventEmitter"></span><span id="431" class="code-item">EventEmitter&lt;T></span>

An event emitter can be used to create and manage an [event](#Event) for others to subscribe to. One emitter always owns one event.

Use this class if you want to provide event from within your extension, for instance inside a [TextDocumentContentProvider](#TextDocumentContentProvider) or when providing API to other extensions.

#### Properties

<span id="EventEmitter.event"></span><span id="433" class="ts" data-target="#details-433" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">event</span>: <a href="#Event" class="type-ref">Event</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>&gt;</span>

The event listeners can subscribe to.

#### Methods

<span id="EventEmitter.dispose"></span><span id="438" class="ts" data-target="#details-438" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">dispose</span>(): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Dispose this object and free resources.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><td><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></td><td><div class="comment"></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="EventEmitter.fire"></span><span id="435" class="ts" data-target="#details-435" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">fire</span>(<span class="ident">data</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Notify all subscribers of the [event](EventEmitter.html#event). Failure of one or more listener will not fail this function call.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="data"></span><span id="436" class="ts" data-target="#details-436" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">data</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">T</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The event object.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="Extension"></span><span id="1034" class="code-item">Extension&lt;T></span>

Represents an extension.

To get an instance of an `Extension` use [getExtension](#extensions.getExtension).

#### Properties

<span id="Extension.exports"></span><span id="1040" class="ts" data-target="#details-1040" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">exports</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span></span>

The public API exported by this extension. It is an invalid action to access this field before this extension has been activated.

<span id="Extension.extensionPath"></span><span id="1037" class="ts" data-target="#details-1037" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">extensionPath</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The absolute file path of the directory containing this extension.

<span id="Extension.id"></span><span id="1036" class="ts" data-target="#details-1036" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">id</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The canonical extension identifier in the form of: `publisher.name`.

<span id="Extension.isActive"></span><span id="1038" class="ts" data-target="#details-1038" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isActive</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

`true` if the extension has been activated.

<span id="Extension.packageJSON"></span><span id="1039" class="ts" data-target="#details-1039" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">packageJSON</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span></span>

The parsed contents of the extension's package.json.

#### Methods

<span id="Extension.activate"></span><span id="1042" class="ts" data-target="#details-1042" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">activate</span>(): <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>&gt;</span>

Activates this extension and returns its public API.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><td><span class="ts"><a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>&gt;</span></td><td><div class="comment"><p>A promise that will resolve when this extension has been activated.</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="ExtensionContext"></span><span id="1043" class="code-item">ExtensionContext</span>

An extension context is a collection of utilities private to an extension.

An instance of an `ExtensionContext` is provided as the first parameter to the `activate`-call of an extension.

#### Properties

<span id="ExtensionContext.extensionPath"></span><span id="1050" class="ts" data-target="#details-1050" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">extensionPath</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The absolute file path of the directory containing the extension.

<span id="ExtensionContext.globalState"></span><span id="1049" class="ts" data-target="#details-1049" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">globalState</span>: <a href="#Memento" class="type-ref">Memento</a></span>

A memento object that stores state independent of the current opened [workspace](#workspace.workspaceFolders).

<span id="ExtensionContext.storagePath"></span><span id="1054" class="ts" data-target="#details-1054" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">storagePath</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

An absolute file path of a workspace specific directory in which the extension can store private state. The directory might not exist on disk and creation is up to the extension. However, the parent directory is guaranteed to be existent.

Use [`workspaceState`](#ExtensionContext.workspaceState) or [`globalState`](#ExtensionContext.globalState) to store key value data.

<span id="ExtensionContext.subscriptions"></span><span id="1044" class="ts" data-target="#details-1044" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">subscriptions</span>: {dispose}\[\]</span>

An array to which disposables can be added. When this extension is deactivated the disposables will be disposed.

<span id="ExtensionContext.workspaceState"></span><span id="1048" class="ts" data-target="#details-1048" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">workspaceState</span>: <a href="#Memento" class="type-ref">Memento</a></span>

A memento object that stores state in the context of the currently opened [workspace](#workspace.workspaceFolders).

#### Methods

<span id="ExtensionContext.asAbsolutePath"></span><span id="1052" class="ts" data-target="#details-1052" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">asAbsolutePath</span>(<span class="ident">relativePath</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Get the absolute path of a resource contained in the extension.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="relativePath"></span><span id="1053" class="ts" data-target="#details-1053" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">relativePath</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A relative path to a resource contained in the extension.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The absolute path of the resource.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="FileSystemWatcher"></span><span id="439" class="code-item">FileSystemWatcher</span>

A file system watcher notifies about changes to files and folders on disk.

To get an instance of a `FileSystemWatcher` use [createFileSystemWatcher](#workspace.createFileSystemWatcher).

#### Events

<span id="FileSystemWatcher.onDidChange"></span><span id="444" class="ts" data-target="#details-444" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">onDidChange</span>: <a href="#Event" class="type-ref">Event</a>&lt;<a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>&gt;</span>

An event which fires on file/folder change.

<span id="FileSystemWatcher.onDidCreate"></span><span id="443" class="ts" data-target="#details-443" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">onDidCreate</span>: <a href="#Event" class="type-ref">Event</a>&lt;<a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>&gt;</span>

An event which fires on file/folder creation.

<span id="FileSystemWatcher.onDidDelete"></span><span id="445" class="ts" data-target="#details-445" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">onDidDelete</span>: <a href="#Event" class="type-ref">Event</a>&lt;<a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>&gt;</span>

An event which fires on file/folder deletion.

#### Static

<span id="FileSystemWatcher.from"></span><span id="447" class="ts" data-target="#details-447" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">from</span>(...<span class="ident">disposableLikes</span>: {dispose: () => <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>}\[\]): <a href="#Disposable" class="type-ref">Disposable</a></span>

Combine many disposable-likes into one. Use this method when having objects with a dispose function which are not instances of Disposable.

### <span id="Hover"></span><span id="540" class="code-item">Hover</span>

A hover represents additional information for a symbol or word. Hovers are rendered in a tooltip-like widget.

#### Constructors

<span id="Hover.new Hover"></span><span id="544" class="ts" data-target="#details-544" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Hover</span>(<span class="ident">contents</span>: <a href="#MarkedString" class="type-ref">MarkedString</a> | <a href="#MarkedString" class="type-ref">MarkedString</a>\[\], <span class="ident">range</span>?: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>): <a href="#Hover" class="type-ref">Hover</a></span>

Creates a new hover object.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="contents"></span><span id="545" class="ts" data-target="#details-545" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">contents</span><span>: </span><a href="#MarkedString" class="type-ref">MarkedString</a> | <a href="#MarkedString" class="type-ref">MarkedString</a>[]</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The contents of the hover.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="range"></span><span id="546" class="ts" data-target="#details-546" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The range to which the hover applies.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Hover" class="type-ref">Hover</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Hover.contents"></span><span id="541" class="ts" data-target="#details-541" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">contents</span>: <a href="#MarkedString" class="type-ref">MarkedString</a>\[\]</span>

The contents of this hover.

<span id="Hover.range"></span><span id="542" class="ts" data-target="#details-542" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span>?: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

The range to which this hover applies. When missing, the editor will use the range at the current position or the current position itself.

### <span id="HoverProvider"></span><span id="547" class="code-item">HoverProvider</span>

The hover provider interface defines the contract between extensions and the [hover](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/intellisense)-feature.

#### Methods

<span id="HoverProvider.provideHover"></span><span id="549" class="ts" data-target="#details-549" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideHover</span>(<span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a>, <span class="ident">position</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Hover" class="type-ref">Hover</a>&gt;</span>

Provide a hover for the given position and document. Multiple hovers at the same position will be merged by the editor. A hover can have a range which defaults to the word range at the position when omitted.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="document"></span><span id="550" class="ts" data-target="#details-550" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">document</span><span>: </span><a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The document in which the command was invoked.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="position"></span><span id="551" class="ts" data-target="#details-551" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">position</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The position at which the command was invoked.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="552" class="ts" data-target="#details-552" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Hover" class="type-ref">Hover</a>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A hover or a thenable that resolves to such. The lack of a result can be signaled by returning <code>undefined</code> or <code>null</code>.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="IndentationRule"></span><span id="849" class="code-item">IndentationRule</span>

Describes indentation rules for a language.

#### Properties

<span id="IndentationRule.decreaseIndentPattern"></span><span id="850" class="ts" data-target="#details-850" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">decreaseIndentPattern</span>: <a href="#RegExp" class="type-ref">RegExp</a></span>

If a line matches this pattern, then all the lines after it should be unindendented once (until another rule matches).

<span id="IndentationRule.increaseIndentPattern"></span><span id="851" class="ts" data-target="#details-851" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">increaseIndentPattern</span>: <a href="#RegExp" class="type-ref">RegExp</a></span>

If a line matches this pattern, then all the lines after it should be indented once (until another rule matches).

<span id="IndentationRule.indentNextLinePattern"></span><span id="852" class="ts" data-target="#details-852" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">indentNextLinePattern</span>?: <a href="#RegExp" class="type-ref">RegExp</a></span>

If a line matches this pattern, then **only the next line** after it should be indented once.

<span id="IndentationRule.unIndentedLinePattern"></span><span id="853" class="ts" data-target="#details-853" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">unIndentedLinePattern</span>?: <a href="#RegExp" class="type-ref">RegExp</a></span>

If a line matches this pattern, then its indentation should not be changed and it should not be evaluated against the other rules.

### <span id="InputBoxOptions"></span><span id="481" class="code-item">InputBoxOptions</span>

Options to configure the behavior of the input box UI.

#### Properties

<span id="InputBoxOptions.ignoreFocusOut"></span><span id="487" class="ts" data-target="#details-487" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">ignoreFocusOut</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Set to `true` to keep the input box open when focus moves to another part of the editor or to another window.

<span id="InputBoxOptions.password"></span><span id="486" class="ts" data-target="#details-486" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">password</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Set to `true` to show a password prompt that will not show the typed value.

<span id="InputBoxOptions.placeHolder"></span><span id="485" class="ts" data-target="#details-485" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">placeHolder</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

An optional string to show as place holder in the input box to guide the user what to type.

<span id="InputBoxOptions.prompt"></span><span id="484" class="ts" data-target="#details-484" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">prompt</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The text to display underneath the input box.

<span id="InputBoxOptions.value"></span><span id="482" class="ts" data-target="#details-482" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The value to prefill in the input box.

<span id="InputBoxOptions.valueSelection"></span><span id="483" class="ts" data-target="#details-483" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">valueSelection</span>?: \[<span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>\]</span>

Selection of the prefilled [`value`](#InputBoxOptions.value). Defined as tuple of two number where the first is the inclusive start index and the second the exclusive end index. When `undefined` the whole word will be selected, when empty (start equals end) only the cursor will be set, otherwise the defined range will be selected.

#### Methods

<span id="InputBoxOptions.validateInput"></span><span id="489" class="ts" data-target="#details-489" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">validateInput</span>(<span class="ident">value</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">null</span></span>

An optional function that will be called to validate input and to give a hint to the user.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="value"></span><span id="490" class="ts" data-target="#details-490" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The current value of the input box.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">null</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A human readable string which is presented as diagnostic message. Return <code>undefined</code>, <code>null</code>, or the empty string when 'value' is valid.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="LanguageConfiguration"></span><span id="867" class="code-item">LanguageConfiguration</span>

The language configuration interfaces defines the contract between extensions and various editor features, like automatic bracket insertion, automatic indentation etc.

#### Properties

<span id="LanguageConfiguration.___characterPairSupport"></span><span id="882" class="ts" data-target="#details-882" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">\_\_\_characterPairSupport</span>?: {autoClosingPairs: {close: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, notIn: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>\[\], open: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>}\[\]}</span>

**Deprecated** Do not use.

- _deprecated_ - \* Use the the autoClosingPairs property in the language configuration file instead.

<span id="LanguageConfiguration.___electricCharacterSupport"></span><span id="873" class="ts" data-target="#details-873" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">\_\_\_electricCharacterSupport</span>?: {brackets: <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>, docComment: {close: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, lineStart: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, open: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, scope: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>}}</span>

**Deprecated** Do not use.

- _deprecated_ - Will be replaced by a better API soon.

<span id="LanguageConfiguration.brackets"></span><span id="869" class="ts" data-target="#details-869" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">brackets</span>?: <a href="#CharacterPair" class="type-ref">CharacterPair</a>\[\]</span>

The language's brackets. This configuration implicitly affects pressing Enter around these brackets.

<span id="LanguageConfiguration.comments"></span><span id="868" class="ts" data-target="#details-868" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">comments</span>?: <a href="#CommentRule" class="type-ref">CommentRule</a></span>

The language's comment settings.

<span id="LanguageConfiguration.indentationRules"></span><span id="871" class="ts" data-target="#details-871" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">indentationRules</span>?: <a href="#IndentationRule" class="type-ref">IndentationRule</a></span>

The language's indentation settings.

<span id="LanguageConfiguration.onEnterRules"></span><span id="872" class="ts" data-target="#details-872" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">onEnterRules</span>?: <a href="#OnEnterRule" class="type-ref">OnEnterRule</a>\[\]</span>

The language's rules to be evaluated when pressing Enter.

<span id="LanguageConfiguration.wordPattern"></span><span id="870" class="ts" data-target="#details-870" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">wordPattern</span>?: <a href="#RegExp" class="type-ref">RegExp</a></span>

The language's word definition. If the language supports Unicode identifiers (e.g. JavaScript), it is preferable to provide a word definition that uses exclusion of known separators. e.g.: A regex that matches anything except known separators (and dot is allowed to occur in a floating point number): /(-?\\d*.\\d\\w*)|(\[^\`~!\\@@#\\%\\^\\&\*()-\\=+\[{\]}|\\;\\:\\'\\"\\,.\\&lt;&gt;\\/\\?\\s\]+)/g

### <span id="MarkedString"></span><span id="1275" class="code-item">MarkedString</span>

MarkedString can be used to render human readable text. It is either a markdown string or a code-block that provides a language and a code snippet. Note that markdown strings will be sanitized - that means html will be escaped.

<span id="MarkedString"></span><span id="1275" class="ts" data-target="#details-1275" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">MarkedString</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | {language: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, value: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>}</span>

### <span id="OnTypeFormattingEditProvider"></span><span id="737" class="code-item">OnTypeFormattingEditProvider</span>

The document formatting provider interface defines the contract between extensions and the formatting-feature.

#### Methods

<span id="OnTypeFormattingEditProvider.provideOnTypeFormattingEdits"></span><span id="739" class="ts" data-target="#details-739" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideOnTypeFormattingEdits</span>(<span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a>, <span class="ident">position</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">ch</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">options</span>: <a href="#FormattingOptions" class="type-ref">FormattingOptions</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#TextEdit" class="type-ref">TextEdit</a>\[\]&gt;</span>

Provide formatting edits after a character has been typed.

The given position and character should hint to the provider what range the position to expand to, like find the matching `{` when `}` has been entered.

### <span id="ParameterInformation"></span><span id="745" class="code-item">ParameterInformation</span>

Represents a parameter of a callable-signature. A parameter can have a label and a doc-comment.

#### Constructors

Creates a new parameter information object.

### <span id="Position"></span><span id="74" class="code-item">Position</span>

Represents a line and character position, such as the position of the cursor.

Position objects are **immutable**. Use the [with](#Position.with) or [translate](#Position.translate) methods to derive new positions from an existing position.

#### Constructors

<span id="Position.new Position"></span><span id="78" class="ts" data-target="#details-78" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Position</span>(<span class="ident">line</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="ident">character</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>): <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span>

### <span id="ProviderResult"></span><span id="1273" class="code-item">ProviderResult</span>

A provider result represents the values a provider, like the [`HoverProvider`](#HoverProvider), may return. For once this is the actual result type `T`, like `Hover`, or a thenable that resolves to that type `T`. In addition, `null` and `undefined` can be returned - either directly or from a thenable.

The snippets below are all valid implementions of the [`HoverProvider`](#HoverProvider):

    let a: HoverProvider = {
        provideHover(doc, pos, token): ProviderResult<Hover> {
            return new Hover('Hello World');
        }
    }

    let b: HoverProvider = {
        provideHover(doc, pos, token): ProviderResult<Hover> {
            return new Promise(resolve => {
                resolve(new Hover('Hello World'));
             });
        }
    }

    let c: HoverProvider = {
        provideHover(doc, pos, token): ProviderResult<Hover> {
            return; // undefined
        }
    }

<span id="ProviderResult"></span><span id="1273" class="ts" data-target="#details-1273" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">ProviderResult</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">null</span> | <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">T</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">null</span>&gt;</span>

### <span id="QuickDiffProvider"></span><span id="1215" class="code-item">QuickDiffProvider</span>

#### Methods

<span id="QuickDiffProvider.provideOriginalResource"></span><span id="1217" class="ts" data-target="#details-1217" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideOriginalResource</span>(<span class="ident">uri</span>: <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>&gt;</span>

Provide a [uri](#Uri) to the original resource of any given resource uri.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="uri"></span><span id="1218" class="ts" data-target="#details-1218" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">uri</span><span>: </span><a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The uri of the resource open in a text editor.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="1219" class="ts" data-target="#details-1219" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A thenable that resolves to uri of the matching original resource.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="QuickPickItem"></span><span id="464" class="code-item">QuickPickItem</span>
