An optional string to show as place holder in the input box to guide the user what to pick on.

### <span id="Range"></span><span id="117" class="code-item">Range</span>

A range represents an ordered pair of two positions. It is guaranteed that [start](#Range.start).isBeforeOrEqual([end](#Range.end))

Range objects are **immutable**. Use the [with](#Range.with), [intersection](#Range.intersection), or [union](#Range.union) methods to derive new ranges from an existing range.

#### Constructors

<span id="Range.new Range"></span><span id="121" class="ts" data-target="#details-121" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Range</span>(<span class="ident">start</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">end</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>): <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

Create a new range from two positions. If `start` is not before or equal to `end`, the values will be swapped.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="start"></span><span id="122" class="ts" data-target="#details-122" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">start</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A position.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="end"></span><span id="123" class="ts" data-target="#details-123" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">end</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A position.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Range.new Range"></span><span id="124" class="ts" data-target="#details-124" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Range</span>(<span class="ident">startLine</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="ident">startCharacter</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="ident">endLine</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="ident">endCharacter</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>): <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

Create a new range from number coordinates. It is a shorter equivalent of using `new Range(new Position(startLine, startCharacter), new Position(endLine, endCharacter))`

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="startLine"></span><span id="125" class="ts" data-target="#details-125" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">startLine</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based line value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="startCharacter"></span><span id="126" class="ts" data-target="#details-126" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">startCharacter</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based character value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="endLine"></span><span id="127" class="ts" data-target="#details-127" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">endLine</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based line value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="endCharacter"></span><span id="128" class="ts" data-target="#details-128" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">endCharacter</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based character value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

#### Properties

<span id="Range.end"></span><span id="119" class="ts" data-target="#details-119" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">end</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span>

The end position. It is after or equal to [start](#Range.start).

<span id="Range.isEmpty"></span><span id="129" class="ts" data-target="#details-129" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isEmpty</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

`true` if `start` and `end` are equal.

<span id="Range.isSingleLine"></span><span id="130" class="ts" data-target="#details-130" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isSingleLine</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

`true` if `start.line` and `end.line` are equal.

<span id="Range.start"></span><span id="118" class="ts" data-target="#details-118" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">start</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span>

The start position. It is before or equal to [end](#Range.end).

#### Methods

<span id="Range.contains"></span><span id="132" class="ts" data-target="#details-132" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">contains</span>(<span class="ident">positionOrRange</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a> | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>): <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Check if a position or a range is contained in this range.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="positionOrRange"></span><span id="133" class="ts" data-target="#details-133" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">positionOrRange</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a> | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A position or a range.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p><code>true</code> if the position or range is inside or equal to this range.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Range.intersection"></span><span id="138" class="ts" data-target="#details-138" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">intersection</span>(<span class="ident">range</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>): <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

Intersect `range` with this range and returns a new range or `undefined` if the ranges have no overlap.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="range"></span><span id="139" class="ts" data-target="#details-139" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A range.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A range of the greater start and smaller end positions. Will return undefined when there is no overlap.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Range.isEqual"></span><span id="135" class="ts" data-target="#details-135" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isEqual</span>(<span class="ident">other</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>): <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Check if `other` equals this range.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="other"></span><span id="136" class="ts" data-target="#details-136" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">other</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A range.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p><code>true</code> when start and end are <a href="#Position.isEqual">equal</a> to start and end of this range.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Range.union"></span><span id="141" class="ts" data-target="#details-141" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">union</span>(<span class="ident">other</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>): <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

Compute the union of `other` with this range.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="other"></span><span id="142" class="ts" data-target="#details-142" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">other</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A range.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A range of smaller start position and the greater end position.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Range.with"></span><span id="144" class="ts" data-target="#details-144" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">with</span>(<span class="ident">start</span>?: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">end</span>?: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>): <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

### <span id="RenameProvider"></span><span id="712" class="code-item">RenameProvider</span>

<span id="RenameProvider.provideRenameEdits"></span><span id="714" class="ts" data-target="#details-714" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideRenameEdits</span>(<span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a>, <span class="ident">position</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">newName</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#WorkspaceEdit" class="type-ref">WorkspaceEdit</a>&gt;</span>

### <span id="Selection"></span><span id="152" class="code-item">Selection</span>

Represents a text selection in an editor.

#### Constructors

<span id="Selection.new Selection"></span><span id="156" class="ts" data-target="#details-156" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Selection</span>(<span class="ident">anchor</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">active</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>): <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a></span>

Create a selection from two postions.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="anchor"></span><span id="157" class="ts" data-target="#details-157" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">anchor</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A position.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="active"></span><span id="158" class="ts" data-target="#details-158" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">active</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A position.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Selection.new Selection"></span><span id="159" class="ts" data-target="#details-159" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new Selection</span>(<span class="ident">anchorLine</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="ident">anchorCharacter</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="ident">activeLine</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>, <span class="ident">activeCharacter</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>): <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a></span>

Create a selection from four coordinates.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="anchorLine"></span><span id="160" class="ts" data-target="#details-160" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">anchorLine</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based line value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="anchorCharacter"></span><span id="161" class="ts" data-target="#details-161" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">anchorCharacter</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based character value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="activeLine"></span><span id="162" class="ts" data-target="#details-162" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">activeLine</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based line value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="activeCharacter"></span><span id="163" class="ts" data-target="#details-163" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">activeCharacter</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A zero-based character value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

#### Properties

<span id="Selection.active"></span><span id="154" class="ts" data-target="#details-154" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">active</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span>

The position of the cursor. This position might be before or after [anchor](#Selection.anchor).

<span id="Selection.anchor"></span><span id="153" class="ts" data-target="#details-153" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">anchor</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span>

The position at which the selection starts. This position might be before or after [active](#Selection.active).

<span id="Selection.end"></span><span id="166" class="ts" data-target="#details-166" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">end</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span>

The end position. It is after or equal to [start](#Range.start).

<span id="Selection.isEmpty"></span><span id="167" class="ts" data-target="#details-167" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isEmpty</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

`true` if `start` and `end` are equal.

<span id="Selection.isReversed"></span><span id="164" class="ts" data-target="#details-164" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isReversed</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

A selection is reversed if [active](#Selection.active).isBefore([anchor](#Selection.anchor)).

<span id="Selection.isSingleLine"></span><span id="168" class="ts" data-target="#details-168" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isSingleLine</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

`true` if `start.line` and `end.line` are equal.

<span id="Selection.start"></span><span id="165" class="ts" data-target="#details-165" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">start</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span>

The start position. It is before or equal to [end](#Range.end).

### <span id="ShellExecutionOptions"></span><span id="1112" class="code-item">ShellExecutionOptions</span>

#### Properties

The current working directory of the executed shell. If omitted the tools current workspace root is used.

<span id="ShellExecutionOptions.env"></span><span id="1116" class="ts" data-target="#details-1116" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">env</span>?: </span>

The additional environment of the executed shell. If omitted the parent process' environment is used. If provided it is merged with the parent process' environment.

<span id="ShellExecutionOptions.executable"></span><span id="1113" class="ts" data-target="#details-1113" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">executable</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

### <span id="SignatureHelp"></span><span id="760" class="code-item">SignatureHelp</span>

Signature help represents the signature of something callable. There can be multiple signatures but only one active and only one active parameter.

#### Properties

<span id="SignatureHelp.activeParameter"></span><span id="763" class="ts" data-target="#details-763" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">activeParameter</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

<span id="SignatureHelp.activeSignature"></span><span id="762" class="ts" data-target="#details-762" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">activeSignature</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The active signature.

<span id="SignatureHelp.signatures"></span><span id="761" class="ts" data-target="#details-761" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">signatures</span>: <a href="#SignatureInformation" class="type-ref">SignatureInformation</a>\[\]</span>

One or more signatures.

### <span id="SignatureHelpProvider"></span><span id="764" class="code-item">SignatureHelpProvider</span>

The signature help provider interface defines the contract between extensions and the [parameter hints](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/intellisense)-feature.

#### Methods

### <span id="SignatureInformation"></span><span id="752" class="code-item">SignatureInformation</span>

Represents the signature of something callable. A signature can have a label, like a function-name, a doc-comment, and a set of parameters.

#### Constructors

Creates a new signature information object.

### <span id="SnippetString"></span><span id="687" class="code-item">SnippetString</span>

A snippet string is a template which allows to insert text and to control the editor cursor when insertion happens.

A snippet can define tab stops and placeholders with `$1`, `$2` and `${3:foo}`. `$0` defines the final tab stop, it defaults to the end of the snippet. Variables are defined with `$name` and `${name:default value}`. The full snippet syntax is documented [here](http://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/userdefinedsnippets#_creating-your-own-snippets).

#### Constructors

<span id="SnippetString.new SnippetString"></span><span id="690" class="ts" data-target="#details-690" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new SnippetString</span>(<span class="ident">value</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span>

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="value"></span><span id="691" class="ts" data-target="#details-691" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

#### Properties

<span id="SnippetString.value"></span><span id="688" class="ts" data-target="#details-688" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The snippet string.

#### Methods

<span id="SnippetString.appendPlaceholder"></span><span id="699" class="ts" data-target="#details-699" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">appendPlaceholder</span>(<span class="ident">value</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | (snippet: <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a>) => <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>, <span class="ident">number</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>): <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span>

Builder-function that appends a placeholder (`${1:value}`) to the [`value`](#SnippetString.value) of this snippet string.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="value"></span><span id="700" class="ts" data-target="#details-700" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | (snippet: <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a>) =&gt; <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The value of this placeholder - either a string or a function with which a nested snippet can be created.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="number"></span><span id="704" class="ts" data-target="#details-704" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">number</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The number of this tabstop, defaults to an auto-incremet value starting at 1.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>This snippet string.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="SnippetString.appendTabstop"></span><span id="696" class="ts" data-target="#details-696" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">appendTabstop</span>(<span class="ident">number</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>): <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span>

<span id="SnippetString.appendText"></span><span id="693" class="ts" data-target="#details-693" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">appendText</span>(<span class="ident">string</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span>

Builder-function that appends the given string to the [`value`](#SnippetString.value) of this snippet string.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="string"></span><span id="694" class="ts" data-target="#details-694" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">string</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A value to append 'as given'. The string will be escaped.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>This snippet string.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="SnippetString.appendVariable"></span><span id="706" class="ts" data-target="#details-706" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">appendVariable</span>(<span class="ident">name</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">defaultValue</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | (snippet: <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a>) => <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>): <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span>

Builder-function that appends a variable (`${VAR}`) to the [`value`](#SnippetString.value) of this snippet string.

### <span id="SourceControl"></span><span id="1239" class="code-item">SourceControl</span>

An source control is able to provide [resource states](#SourceControlResourceState) to the editor and interact with the editor in several source control related ways.

#### Properties

<span id="SourceControl.acceptInputCommand"></span><span id="1245" class="ts" data-target="#details-1245" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">acceptInputCommand</span>?: <a href="#Command" class="type-ref">Command</a></span>

Optional accept input command.

This command will be invoked when the user accepts the value in the Source Control input.

<span id="SourceControl.commitTemplate"></span><span id="1244" class="ts" data-target="#details-1244" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">commitTemplate</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Optional commit template string.

The Source Control viewlet will populate the Source Control input with this value when appropriate.

<span id="SourceControl.count"></span><span id="1242" class="ts" data-target="#details-1242" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">count</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The UI-visible count of [resource states](#SourceControlResourceState) of this source control.

Equals to the total number of [resource state](#SourceControlResourceState) of this source control, if undefined.

<span id="SourceControl.id"></span><span id="1240" class="ts" data-target="#details-1240" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">id</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The id of this source control.

<span id="SourceControl.label"></span><span id="1241" class="ts" data-target="#details-1241" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">label</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The human-readable label of this source control.

<span id="SourceControl.quickDiffProvider"></span><span id="1243" class="ts" data-target="#details-1243" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">quickDiffProvider</span>?: <a href="#QuickDiffProvider" class="type-ref">QuickDiffProvider</a></span>

An optional [quick diff provider](#QuickDiffProvider).

<span id="SourceControl.statusBarCommands"></span><span id="1246" class="ts" data-target="#details-1246" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">statusBarCommands</span>?: <a href="#Command" class="type-ref">Command</a>\[\]</span>

Optional status bar commands.

These commands will be displayed in the editor's status bar.

#### Methods

<span id="SourceControl.createResourceGroup"></span><span id="1248" class="ts" data-target="#details-1248" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">createResourceGroup</span>(<span class="ident">id</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">label</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <a href="#SourceControlResourceGroup" class="type-ref">SourceControlResourceGroup</a></span>

### <span id="StatusBarItem"></span><span id="1002" class="code-item">StatusBarItem</span>

A status bar item is a status bar contribution that can show text and icons and run a command on click.

#### Properties

<span id="StatusBarItem.alignment"></span><span id="1003" class="ts" data-target="#details-1003" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">alignment</span>: <span class="type-unknown">StatusBarAlignment.Left</span> | <span class="type-unknown">StatusBarAlignment.Right</span></span>

The alignment of this item.

<span id="StatusBarItem.color"></span><span id="1007" class="ts" data-target="#details-1007" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">color</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

The foreground color for this entry.

<span id="StatusBarItem.command"></span><span id="1008" class="ts" data-target="#details-1008" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">command</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

The identifier of a command to run on click. The command must be [known](#commands.getCommands).

<span id="StatusBarItem.priority"></span><span id="1004" class="ts" data-target="#details-1004" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">priority</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The priority of this item. Higher value means the item should be shown more to the left.

<span id="StatusBarItem.text"></span><span id="1005" class="ts" data-target="#details-1005" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">text</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The text to show for the entry. You can embed icons in the text by leveraging the syntax:

`My text $(icon-name) contains icons like $(icon'name) this one.`

Where the icon-name is taken from the [octicon](https://octicons.github.com/) icon set, e.g. `light-bulb`, `thumbsup`, `zap` etc.

<span id="StatusBarItem.tooltip"></span><span id="1006" class="ts" data-target="#details-1006" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">tooltip</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

The tooltip text when you hover over this entry.

#### Methods

<span id="StatusBarItem.dispose"></span><span id="1014" class="ts" data-target="#details-1014" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">dispose</span>(): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Dispose and free associated resources. Call [hide](#StatusBarItem.hide).

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><td><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></td><td><div class="comment"></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

A task to execute

Creates a new task.

<span id="Task.execution"></span><span id="1137" class="ts" data-target="#details-1137" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">execution</span>: <a href="#ProcessExecution" class="type-ref">ProcessExecution</a> | <a href="#ShellExecution" class="type-ref">ShellExecution</a></span>

<span id="Task.group"></span><span id="1140" class="ts" data-target="#details-1140" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">group</span>?: <a href="#TaskGroup" class="type-ref">TaskGroup</a></span>

A human-readable string describing the source of this shell task, e.g. 'gulp' or 'npm'.

### <span id="TaskDefinition"></span><span id="1090" class="code-item">TaskDefinition</span>

A structure that defines a task kind in the system. The value must be JSON-stringifyable.

#### Properties

<span id="TaskDefinition.type"></span><span id="1091" class="ts" data-target="#details-1091" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">type</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The task definition descibing the task provided by an extension. Usually a task provider defines more properties to identify a task. They need to be defined in the package.json of the extension under the 'taskDefinitions' extension point. The npm task definition for example looks like this

    interface NpmTaskDefinition extends TaskDefinition {
        script: string;
    }

### <span id="TaskGroup"></span><span id="1081" class="code-item">TaskGroup</span>

### <span id="TaskPresentationOptions"></span><span id="1076" class="code-item">TaskPresentationOptions</span>

#### Properties

<span id="TaskPresentationOptions.echo"></span><span id="1078" class="ts" data-target="#details-1078" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">echo</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Controls whether the command associated with the task is echoed in the user interface.

<span id="TaskPresentationOptions.focus"></span><span id="1079" class="ts" data-target="#details-1079" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">focus</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Controls whether the panel showing the task output is taking focus.

<span id="TaskPresentationOptions.panel"></span><span id="1080" class="ts" data-target="#details-1080" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">panel</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">TaskPanelKind.Shared</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TaskPanelKind.Dedicated</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TaskPanelKind.New</span></span>

Controls if the task panel is used for this task only (dedicated), shared between tasks (shared) or if a new panel is created on every task execution (new). Defaults to `TaskInstanceKind.Shared`

<span id="TaskPresentationOptions.reveal"></span><span id="1077" class="ts" data-target="#details-1077" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">reveal</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">TaskRevealKind.Always</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TaskRevealKind.Silent</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TaskRevealKind.Never</span></span>

Controls whether the task output is reveal in the user interface. Defaults to `RevealKind.Always`.

### <span id="TaskProvider"></span><span id="1143" class="code-item">TaskProvider</span>

A task provider allows to add tasks to the task service. A task provider is registerd via #workspace.registerTaskProvider.

#### Methods

<span id="TaskProvider.provideTasks"></span><span id="1145" class="ts" data-target="#details-1145" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideTasks</span>(<span class="ident">token</span>?: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Task" class="type-ref">Task</a>\[\]&gt;</span>

Provides tasks.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="1146" class="ts" data-target="#details-1146" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Task" class="type-ref">Task</a>[]&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>an array of tasks</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TaskProvider.resolveTask"></span><span id="1148" class="ts" data-target="#details-1148" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">resolveTask</span>(<span class="ident">task</span>: <a href="#Task" class="type-ref">Task</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>?: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Task" class="type-ref">Task</a>&gt;</span>

Resolves a task that has no [`execution`](#Task.execution) set. Tasks are often created from information found in the `task.json`-file. Such tasks miss the information on how to execute them and a task provider must fill in the missing information in the `resolveTask`-method.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="task"></span><span id="1149" class="ts" data-target="#details-1149" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">task</span><span>: </span><a href="#Task" class="type-ref">Task</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The task to resolve.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="1150" class="ts" data-target="#details-1150" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#Task" class="type-ref">Task</a>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The resolved task</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="Terminal"></span><span id="1020" class="code-item">Terminal</span>

An individual terminal instance within the integrated terminal.

#### Properties

<span id="Terminal.name"></span><span id="1021" class="ts" data-target="#details-1021" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">name</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

<span id="Terminal.processId"></span><span id="1022" class="ts" data-target="#details-1022" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">processId</span>: <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>&gt;</span>

#### Methods

<span id="Terminal.dispose"></span><span id="1033" class="ts" data-target="#details-1033" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">dispose</span>(): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><td><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></td><td><div class="comment"></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Terminal.hide"></span><span id="1031" class="ts" data-target="#details-1031" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">hide</span>(): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Hide the terminal panel if this terminal is currently showing.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><td><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></td><td><div class="comment"></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Terminal.sendText"></span><span id="1024" class="ts" data-target="#details-1024" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">sendText</span>(<span class="ident">text</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">addNewLine</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Send text to the terminal. The text is written to the stdin of the underlying pty process (shell) of the terminal.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="text"></span><span id="1025" class="ts" data-target="#details-1025" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">text</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The text to send.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="addNewLine"></span><span id="1026" class="ts" data-target="#details-1026" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">addNewLine</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Whether to add a new line to the text being sent, this is normally required to run a command in the terminal. The character(s) added are \n or \r\n depending on the platform. This defaults to <code>true</code>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Terminal.show"></span><span id="1028" class="ts" data-target="#details-1028" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">show</span>(<span class="ident">preserveFocus</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Show the terminal panel and reveal this terminal in the UI.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="preserveFocus"></span><span id="1029" class="ts" data-target="#details-1029" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">preserveFocus</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>When <code>true</code> the terminal will not take focus.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="TerminalOptions"></span><span id="1177" class="code-item">TerminalOptions</span>

Value-object describing what options a terminal should use.

#### Properties

<span id="TerminalOptions.name"></span><span id="1178" class="ts" data-target="#details-1178" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">name</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

A human-readable string which will be used to represent the terminal in the UI.

<span id="TerminalOptions.shellArgs"></span><span id="1180" class="ts" data-target="#details-1180" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">shellArgs</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>\[\]</span>

Args for the custom shell executable, this does not work on Windows (see #8429)

<span id="TerminalOptions.shellPath"></span><span id="1179" class="ts" data-target="#details-1179" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">shellPath</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

### <span id="TextDocument"></span><span id="38" class="code-item">TextDocument</span>

Represents a text document, such as a source file. Text documents have [lines](#TextLine) and knowledge about an underlying resource like a file.

#### Properties

<span id="TextDocument.eol"></span><span id="48" class="ts" data-target="#details-48" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">eol</span>: <span class="type-unknown">EndOfLine.LF</span> | <span class="type-unknown">EndOfLine.CRLF</span></span>

The [end of line](#EndOfLine) sequence that is predominately used in this document.

<span id="TextDocument.fileName"></span><span id="40" class="ts" data-target="#details-40" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">fileName</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The file system path of the associated resource. Shorthand notation for [TextDocument.uri.fsPath](#TextDocument.uri). Independent of the uri scheme.

<span id="TextDocument.isClosed"></span><span id="45" class="ts" data-target="#details-45" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isClosed</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

`true` if the document have been closed. A closed document isn't synchronized anymore and won't be re-used when the same resource is opened again.

<span id="TextDocument.isDirty"></span><span id="44" class="ts" data-target="#details-44" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isDirty</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

`true` if there are unpersisted changes.

<span id="TextDocument.isUntitled"></span><span id="41" class="ts" data-target="#details-41" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isUntitled</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Is this document representing an untitled file.

<span id="TextDocument.languageId"></span><span id="42" class="ts" data-target="#details-42" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">languageId</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The identifier of the language associated with this document.

<span id="TextDocument.lineCount"></span><span id="49" class="ts" data-target="#details-49" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">lineCount</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The number of lines in this document.

<span id="TextDocument.uri"></span><span id="39" class="ts" data-target="#details-39" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">uri</span>: <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span>

The associated URI for this document. Most documents have the **file**-scheme, indicating that they represent files on disk. However, some documents may have other schemes indicating that they are not available on disk.

<span id="TextDocument.version"></span><span id="43" class="ts" data-target="#details-43" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">version</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The version number of this document (it will strictly increase after each change, including undo/redo).

#### Methods

<span id="TextDocument.getText"></span><span id="62" class="ts" data-target="#details-62" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">getText</span>(<span class="ident">range</span>?: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>): <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Get the text of this document. A substring can be retrieved by providing a range. The range will be [adjusted](#TextDocument.validateRange).

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="range"></span><span id="63" class="ts" data-target="#details-63" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Include only the text included by the range.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The text inside the provided range or the entire text.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextDocument.getWordRangeAtPosition"></span><span id="65" class="ts" data-target="#details-65" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">getWordRangeAtPosition</span>(<span class="ident">position</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">regex</span>?: <a href="#RegExp" class="type-ref">RegExp</a>): <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

Get a word-range at the given position. By default words are defined by common separators, like space, -, \_, etc. In addition, per languge custom [word definitions](#LanguageConfiguration.wordPattern) can be defined. It is also possible to provide a custom regular expression.

- _Note 1:_ A custom regular expression must not match the empty string and if it does, it will be ignored.
- _Note 2:_ A custom regular expression will fail to match multiline strings and in the name of speed regular expressions should not match words with spaces. Use [`TextLine.text`](#TextLine.text) for more complex, non-wordy, scenarios.

The position will be [adjusted](#TextDocument.validatePosition).

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="position"></span><span id="66" class="ts" data-target="#details-66" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">position</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A position.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="regex"></span><span id="67" class="ts" data-target="#details-67" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">regex</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><a href="#RegExp" class="type-ref">RegExp</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Optional regular expression that describes what a word is.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A range spanning a word, or <code>undefined</code>.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextDocument.lineAt"></span><span id="51" class="ts" data-target="#details-51" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">lineAt</span>(<span class="ident">line</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span>): <a href="#TextLine" class="type-ref">TextLine</a></span>

Returns a text line denoted by the line number. Note that the returned object is _not_ live and changes to the document are not reflected.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="line"></span><span id="52" class="ts" data-target="#details-52" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">line</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A line number in [0, lineCount).</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#TextLine" class="type-ref">TextLine</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A <a href="#TextLine">line</a>.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextDocument.lineAt"></span><span id="53" class="ts" data-target="#details-53" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">lineAt</span>(<span class="ident">position</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>): <a href="#TextLine" class="type-ref">TextLine</a></span>

### <span id="TextDocumentContentProvider"></span><span id="458" class="code-item">TextDocumentContentProvider</span>

A text document content provider allows to add readonly documents to the editor, such as source from a dll or generated html from md.

Content providers are [registered](#workspace.registerTextDocumentContentProvider) for a [uri-scheme](#Uri.scheme). When a uri with that scheme is to be [loaded](#workspace.openTextDocument) the content provider is asked.

#### Events

<span id="TextDocumentContentProvider.onDidChange"></span><span id="459" class="ts" data-target="#details-459" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">onDidChange</span>?: <a href="#Event" class="type-ref">Event</a>&lt;<a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>&gt;</span>

An event to signal a resource has changed.

#### Methods

<span id="TextDocumentContentProvider.provideTextDocumentContent"></span><span id="461" class="ts" data-target="#details-461" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideTextDocumentContent</span>(<span class="ident">uri</span>: <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>&gt;</span>

Provide textual content for a given uri.

The editor will use the returned string-content to create a readonly [document](#TextDocument). Resources allocated should be released when the corresponding document has been [closed](#workspace.onDidCloseTextDocument).

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="uri"></span><span id="462" class="ts" data-target="#details-462" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">uri</span><span>: </span><a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>An uri which scheme matches the scheme this provider was <a href="#workspace.registerTextDocumentContentProvider">registered</a> for.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="463" class="ts" data-target="#details-463" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A string or a thenable that resolves to such.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="TextDocumentShowOptions"></span><span id="239" class="code-item">TextDocumentShowOptions</span>

Represents options to configure the behavior of showing a [document](#TextDocument) in an [editor](#TextEditor).

#### Properties

<span id="TextDocumentShowOptions.preserveFocus"></span><span id="241" class="ts" data-target="#details-241" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">preserveFocus</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

An optional flag that when `true` will stop the [editor](#TextEditor) from taking focus.

<span id="TextDocumentShowOptions.preview"></span><span id="242" class="ts" data-target="#details-242" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">preview</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

An optional flag that controls if an [editor](#TextEditor)-tab will be replaced with the next editor or if it will be kept.

<span id="TextDocumentShowOptions.selection"></span><span id="243" class="ts" data-target="#details-243" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">selection</span>?: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

<span id="TextDocumentShowOptions.viewColumn"></span><span id="240" class="ts" data-target="#details-240" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">viewColumn</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">ViewColumn.One</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ViewColumn.Two</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ViewColumn.Three</span></span>

An optional view column in which the [editor](#TextEditor) should be shown. The default is the [one](#ViewColumn.One), other values are adjusted to be **Min(column, columnCount + 1)**.

### <span id="TextDocumentWillSaveEvent"></span><span id="1198" class="code-item">TextDocumentWillSaveEvent</span>

An event that is fired when a [document](#TextDocument) will be saved.

To make modifications to the document before it is being saved, call the [`waitUntil`](#TextDocumentWillSaveEvent.waitUntil)-function with a thenable that resolves to an array of [text edits](#TextEdit).

#### Properties

<span id="TextDocumentWillSaveEvent.document"></span><span id="1199" class="ts" data-target="#details-1199" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a></span>

The document that will be saved.

<span id="TextDocumentWillSaveEvent.reason"></span><span id="1200" class="ts" data-target="#details-1200" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">reason</span>: <span class="type-unknown">TextDocumentSaveReason.Manual</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextDocumentSaveReason.AfterDelay</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextDocumentSaveReason.FocusOut</span></span>

The reason why save was triggered.

#### Methods

<span id="TextDocumentWillSaveEvent.waitUntil"></span><span id="1202" class="ts" data-target="#details-1202" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">waitUntil</span>(<span class="ident">thenable</span>: <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<a href="#TextEdit" class="type-ref">TextEdit</a>\[\]&gt;): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Allows to pause the event loop and to apply [pre-save-edits](#TextEdit). Edits of subsequent calls to this function will be applied in order. The edits will be _ignored_ if concurrent modifications of the document happened.

_Note:_ This function can only be called during event dispatch and not in an asynchronous manner:

    workspace.onWillSaveTextDocument(event => {
        // async, will *throw* an error
        setTimeout(() => event.waitUntil(promise));

        // sync, OK
        event.waitUntil(promise);
    })

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="thenable"></span><span id="1203" class="ts" data-target="#details-1203" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">thenable</span><span>: </span><a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<a href="#TextEdit" class="type-ref">TextEdit</a>[]&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A thenable that resolves to <a href="#TextEdit">pre-save-edits</a>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextDocumentWillSaveEvent.waitUntil"></span><span id="1204" class="ts" data-target="#details-1204" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">waitUntil</span>(<span class="ident">thenable</span>: <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>&gt;): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Allows to pause the event loop until the provided thenable resolved.

_Note:_ This function can only be called during event dispatch.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="thenable"></span><span id="1205" class="ts" data-target="#details-1205" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">thenable</span><span>: </span><a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A thenable that delays saving.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="TextEdit"></span><span id="637" class="code-item">TextEdit</span>

A text edit represents edits that should be applied to a document.

#### Static

### <span id="TextEditor"></span><span id="318" class="code-item">TextEditor</span>

Represents an editor that is attached to a [document](#TextDocument).

#### Properties

<span id="TextEditor.document"></span><span id="319" class="ts" data-target="#details-319" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">document</span>: <a href="#TextDocument" class="type-ref">TextDocument</a></span>

The document associated with this text editor. The document will be the same for the entire lifetime of this text editor.

<span id="TextEditor.options"></span><span id="322" class="ts" data-target="#details-322" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">options</span>: <a href="#TextEditorOptions" class="type-ref">TextEditorOptions</a></span>

Text editor options.

<span id="TextEditor.selection"></span><span id="320" class="ts" data-target="#details-320" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">selection</span>: <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a></span>

The primary selection on this text editor. Shorthand for `TextEditor.selections[0]`.

<span id="TextEditor.selections"></span><span id="321" class="ts" data-target="#details-321" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">selections</span>: <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a>\[\]</span>

The selections in this text editor. The primary selection is always at index 0.

<span id="TextEditor.viewColumn"></span><span id="323" class="ts" data-target="#details-323" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">viewColumn</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">ViewColumn.One</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ViewColumn.Two</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ViewColumn.Three</span></span>

The column in which this editor shows. Will be `undefined` in case this isn't one of the three main editors, e.g an embedded editor.

#### Methods

<span id="TextEditor.edit"></span><span id="325" class="ts" data-target="#details-325" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">edit</span>(<span class="ident">callback</span>: (editBuilder: <a href="#TextEditorEdit" class="type-ref">TextEditorEdit</a>) => <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span>, <span class="ident">options</span>?: {undoStopAfter: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>, undoStopBefore: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>}): <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>&gt;</span>

Perform an edit on the document associated with this text editor.

The given callback-function is invoked with an [edit-builder](#TextEditorEdit) which must be used to make edits. Note that the edit-builder is only valid while the callback executes.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="callback"></span><span id="326" class="ts" data-target="#details-326" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">callback</span><span>: </span>(editBuilder: <a href="#TextEditorEdit" class="type-ref">TextEditorEdit</a>) =&gt; <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A function which can create edits using an <a href="#TextEditorEdit">edit-builder</a>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="options"></span><span id="330" class="ts" data-target="#details-330" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">options</span><span>?</span><span>: </span>{undoStopAfter: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>, undoStopBefore: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>}</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The undo/redo behavior around this edit. By default, undo stops will be created before and after this edit.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A promise that resolves with a value indicating if the edits could be applied.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextEditor.hide"></span><span id="354" class="ts" data-target="#details-354" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">hide</span>(): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

<s>Hide the text editor.</s>

- _deprecated_ - Use the command `workbench.action.closeActiveEditor` instead. This method shows unexpected behavior and will be removed in the next major update.

<span id="TextEditor.insertSnippet"></span><span id="335" class="ts" data-target="#details-335" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">insertSnippet</span>(<span class="ident">snippet</span>: <a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a>, <span class="ident">location</span>?: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a> | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>\[\] | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>\[\], <span class="ident">options</span>?: {undoStopAfter: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>, undoStopBefore: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>}): <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>&gt;</span>

Insert a [snippet](#SnippetString) and put the editor into snippet mode. "Snippet mode" means the editor adds placeholders and additionals cursors so that the user can complete or accept the snippet.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="snippet"></span><span id="336" class="ts" data-target="#details-336" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">snippet</span><span>: </span><a href="#SnippetString" class="type-ref">SnippetString</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The snippet to insert in this edit.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="location"></span><span id="337" class="ts" data-target="#details-337" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">location</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a> | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>[] | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a>[]</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Position or range at which to insert the snippet, defaults to the current editor selection or selections.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="options"></span><span id="338" class="ts" data-target="#details-338" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">options</span><span>?</span><span>: </span>{undoStopAfter: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>, undoStopBefore: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>}</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The undo/redo behavior around this edit. ### <span id="TextEditorDecorationType"></span><span id="220" class="code-item">TextEditorDecorationType</span>

Represents a handle to a set of decorations sharing the same [styling options](#DecorationRenderOptions) in a [text editor](#TextEditor).

To get an instance of a `TextEditorDecorationType` use [createTextEditorDecorationType](#window.createTextEditorDecorationType).

Remove this decoration type and all decorations on all text editors using it.

### <span id="TextEditorEdit"></span><span id="358" class="code-item">TextEditorEdit</span>

A complex edit that will be applied in one transaction on a TextEditor. This holds a description of the edits and if the edits are valid (i.e. no overlapping regions, document was not changed in the meantime, etc.) they can be applied on a [document](#TextDocument) associated with a [text editor](#TextEditor).

#### Methods

<span id="TextEditorEdit.delete"></span><span id="368" class="ts" data-target="#details-368" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">delete</span>(<span class="ident">location</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Delete a certain text region.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="location"></span><span id="369" class="ts" data-target="#details-369" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">location</span><span>: </span><a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The range this operation should remove.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextEditorEdit.insert"></span><span id="364" class="ts" data-target="#details-364" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">insert</span>(<span class="ident">location</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a>, <span class="ident">value</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Insert text at a location. You can use \\r\\n or \\n in `value` and they will be normalized to the current [document](#TextDocument). Although the equivalent text edit can be made with [replace](#TextEditorEdit.replace), `insert` will produce a different resulting selection (it will get moved).

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="location"></span><span id="365" class="ts" data-target="#details-365" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">location</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The position where the new text should be inserted.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="value"></span><span id="366" class="ts" data-target="#details-366" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The new text this operation should insert.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextEditorEdit.replace"></span><span id="360" class="ts" data-target="#details-360" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">replace</span>(<span class="ident">location</span>: <a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a> | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a>, <span class="ident">value</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

Replace a certain text region with a new value. You can use \\r\\n or \\n in `value` and they will be normalized to the current [document](#TextDocument).

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="location"></span><span id="361" class="ts" data-target="#details-361" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">location</span><span>: </span><a href="#Position" class="type-ref">Position</a> | <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a> | <a href="#Selection" class="type-ref">Selection</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The range this operation should remove.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="value"></span><span id="362" class="ts" data-target="#details-362" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The new text this operation should insert after removing <code>location</code>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="TextEditorEdit.setEndOfLine"></span><span id="371" class="ts" data-target="#details-371" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">setEndOfLine</span>(<span class="ident">endOfLine</span>: <span class="type-unknown">EndOfLine.LF</span> | <span class="type-unknown">EndOfLine.CRLF</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span>

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="endOfLine"></span><span id="372" class="ts" data-target="#details-372" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">endOfLine</span><span>: </span><span class="type-unknown">EndOfLine.LF</span> | <span class="type-unknown">EndOfLine.CRLF</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The new end of line for the <a href="#TextDocument">document</a>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">void</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="TextEditorOptions"></span><span id="215" class="code-item">TextEditorOptions</span>

Represents a [text editor](#TextEditor)'s [options](#TextEditor.options).

#### Properties

<span id="TextEditorOptions.cursorStyle"></span><span id="218" class="ts" data-target="#details-218" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">cursorStyle</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorCursorStyle.Line</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorCursorStyle.Block</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorCursorStyle.Underline</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorCursorStyle.LineThin</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorCursorStyle.BlockOutline</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorCursorStyle.UnderlineThin</span></span>

The rendering style of the cursor in this editor. When getting a text editor's options, this property will always be present. When setting a text editor's options, this property is optional.

<span id="TextEditorOptions.insertSpaces"></span><span id="217" class="ts" data-target="#details-217" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">insertSpaces</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

When pressing Tab insert [n](#TextEditorOptions.tabSize) spaces. When getting a text editor's options, this property will always be a boolean (resolved). When setting a text editor's options, this property is optional and it can be a boolean or `"auto"`.

<span id="TextEditorOptions.lineNumbers"></span><span id="219" class="ts" data-target="#details-219" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">lineNumbers</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorLineNumbersStyle.Off</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorLineNumbersStyle.On</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TextEditorLineNumbersStyle.Relative</span></span>

Render relative line numbers w.r.t. the current line number. When getting a text editor's options, this property will always be present. When setting a text editor's options, this property is optional.

<span id="TextEditorOptions.tabSize"></span><span id="216" class="ts" data-target="#details-216" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">tabSize</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The size in spaces a tab takes. This is used for two purposes:

- the rendering width of a tab character;
- the number of spaces to insert when [insertSpaces](#TextEditorOptions.insertSpaces) is true.

When getting a text editor's options, this property will always be a number (resolved). When setting a text editor's options, this property is optional and it can be a number or `"auto"`.

### <span id="TextLine"></span><span id="31" class="code-item">TextLine</span>

Represents a line of text, such as a line of source code.

TextLine objects are **immutable**. When a [document](#TextDocument) changes, previously retrieved lines will not represent the latest state.

#### Properties

<span id="TextLine.firstNonWhitespaceCharacterIndex"></span><span id="36" class="ts" data-target="#details-36" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">firstNonWhitespaceCharacterIndex</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The offset of the first character which is not a whitespace character as defined by `/\s/`. **Note** that if a line is all whitespaces the length of the line is returned.

<span id="TextLine.isEmptyOrWhitespace"></span><span id="37" class="ts" data-target="#details-37" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">isEmptyOrWhitespace</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Whether this line is whitespace only, shorthand for [TextLine.firstNonWhitespaceCharacterIndex](#TextLine.firstNonWhitespaceCharacterIndex) === [TextLine.text.length](#TextLine.text).

<span id="TextLine.lineNumber"></span><span id="32" class="ts" data-target="#details-32" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">lineNumber</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The zero-based line number.

<span id="TextLine.range"></span><span id="34" class="ts" data-target="#details-34" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">range</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

The range this line covers without the line separator characters.

<span id="TextLine.rangeIncludingLineBreak"></span><span id="35" class="ts" data-target="#details-35" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">rangeIncludingLineBreak</span>: <a href="#Range" class="type-ref">Range</a></span>

The range this line covers with the line separator characters.

<span id="TextLine.text"></span><span id="33" class="ts" data-target="#details-33" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">text</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The text of this line without the line separator characters.
