### <span id="ThemeColor"></span><span id="244" class="code-item">ThemeColor</span>

A reference to one of the workbench colors as defined in <https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/getstarted/theme-color-reference>. Using a theme color is preferred over a custom color as it gives theme authors and users the possibility to change the color.

#### Constructors

<span id="ThemeColor.new ThemeColor"></span><span id="246" class="ts" data-target="#details-246" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new ThemeColor</span>(<span class="ident">id</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a></span>

Creates a reference to a theme color.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="id"></span><span id="247" class="ts" data-target="#details-247" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">id</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>of the color. The available colors are listed in <a href="https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/getstarted/theme-color-reference">https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/getstarted/theme-color-reference</a>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ThemeColor" class="type-ref">ThemeColor</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="TreeDataProvider"></span><span id="1151" class="code-item">TreeDataProvider&lt;T></span>

A data provider that provides tree data

#### Events

<span id="TreeDataProvider.onDidChangeTreeData"></span><span id="1153" class="ts" data-target="#details-1153" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">onDidChangeTreeData</span>?: <a href="#Event" class="type-ref">Event</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">T</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">null</span>&gt;</span>

An optional event to signal that an element or root has changed. To signal that root has changed, do not pass any argument or pass `undefined` or `null`.

#### Methods

<span id="TreeDataProvider.getChildren"></span><span id="1158" class="ts" data-target="#details-1158" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">getChildren</span>(<span class="ident">element</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>\[\]&gt;</span>

Get the children of `element` or root if no element is passed.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="element"></span><span id="1159" class="ts" data-target="#details-1159" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">element</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">T</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The element from which the provider gets children. Can be <code>undefined</code>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>[]&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Children of <code>element</code> or root if no element is passed.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="TreeItem"></span><span id="1160" class="code-item">TreeItem</span>

#### Constructors

<span id="TreeItem.new TreeItem"></span><span id="1170" class="ts" data-target="#details-1170" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">new TreeItem</span>(<span class="ident">label</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">collapsibleState</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.None</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.Expanded</span>): <a href="#TreeItem" class="type-ref">TreeItem</a></span>

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="label"></span><span id="1171" class="ts" data-target="#details-1171" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">label</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A human-readable string describing this item</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="collapsibleState"></span><span id="1172" class="ts" data-target="#details-1172" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">collapsibleState</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.None</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.Expanded</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>(#TreeItemCollapsibleState) of the tree item. #### Properties

<span id="TreeItem.collapsibleState"></span><span id="1167" class="ts" data-target="#details-1167" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">collapsibleState</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.None</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.Collapsed</span> | <span class="type-unknown">TreeItemCollapsibleState.Expanded</span></span>

[TreeItemCollapsibleState](#TreeItemCollapsibleState) of the tree item.

<span id="TreeItem.command"></span><span id="1166" class="ts" data-target="#details-1166" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">command</span>?: <a href="#Command" class="type-ref">Command</a></span>

The [command](#Command) which should be run when the tree item is selected.

<span id="TreeItem.contextValue"></span><span id="1168" class="ts" data-target="#details-1168" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">contextValue</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Context value of the tree item. This can be used to contribute item specific actions in the tree. For example, a tree item is given a context value as `folder`. When contributing actions to `view/item/context` using `menus` extension point, you can specify context value for key `viewItem` in `when` expression like `viewItem == folder`.

        "contributes": {
            "menus": {
                "view/item/context": [
                    {
                        "command": "extension.deleteFolder",
                        "when": "viewItem == folder"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

This will show action `extension.deleteFolder` only for items with `contextValue` is `folder`.

<span id="TreeItem.iconPath"></span><span id="1162" class="ts" data-target="#details-1162" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">iconPath</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a> | {dark: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>, light: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span> | <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a>}</span>

The icon path for the tree item

### <span id="Uri"></span><span id="373" class="code-item">Uri</span>

A universal resource identifier representing either a file on disk or another resource, like untitled resources.

#### Static

<span id="Uri.file"></span><span id="375" class="ts" data-target="#details-375" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">file</span>(<span class="ident">path</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span>

Create an URI from a file system path. The [scheme](#Uri.scheme) will be `file`.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="path"></span><span id="376" class="ts" data-target="#details-376" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">path</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A file system or UNC path.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A new Uri instance.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Uri.parse"></span><span id="378" class="ts" data-target="#details-378" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">parse</span>(<span class="ident">value</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span>

Create an URI from a string. Will throw if the given value is not valid.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="value"></span><span id="379" class="ts" data-target="#details-379" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The string value of an Uri.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A new Uri instance.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

#### Properties

<span id="Uri.authority"></span><span id="381" class="ts" data-target="#details-381" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">authority</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Authority is the `www.msft.com` part of `http://www.msft.com/some/path?query#fragment`. The part between the first double slashes and the next slash.

<span id="Uri.fragment"></span><span id="384" class="ts" data-target="#details-384" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">fragment</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Fragment is the `fragment` part of `http://www.msft.com/some/path?query#fragment`.

<span id="Uri.fsPath"></span><span id="385" class="ts" data-target="#details-385" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">fsPath</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The string representing the corresponding file system path of this Uri.

Will handle UNC paths and normalize windows drive letters to lower-case. Also uses the platform specific path separator. Will _not_ validate the path for invalid characters and semantics. Will _not_ look at the scheme of this Uri.

<span id="Uri.path"></span><span id="382" class="ts" data-target="#details-382" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">path</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Path is the `/some/path` part of `http://www.msft.com/some/path?query#fragment`.

<span id="Uri.query"></span><span id="383" class="ts" data-target="#details-383" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">query</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Query is the `query` part of `http://www.msft.com/some/path?query#fragment`.

<span id="Uri.scheme"></span><span id="380" class="ts" data-target="#details-380" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">scheme</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Scheme is the `http` part of `http://www.msft.com/some/path?query#fragment`. The part before the first colon.

#### Methods

<span id="Uri.toJSON"></span><span id="399" class="ts" data-target="#details-399" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">toJSON</span>(): <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span></span>

Returns a JSON representation of this Uri.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><td><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">any</span></span></td><td><div class="comment"><p>An object.</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Uri.toString"></span><span id="396" class="ts" data-target="#details-396" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">toString</span>(<span class="ident">skipEncoding</span>?: <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

Returns a string representation of this Uri. The representation and normalization of a URI depends on the scheme. The resulting string can be safely used with [Uri.parse](#Uri.parse).

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="skipEncoding"></span><span id="397" class="ts" data-target="#details-397" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">skipEncoding</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Do not percentage-encode the result, defaults to <code>false</code>. Note that the <code>#</code> and <code>?</code> characters occuring in the path will always be encoded.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A string representation of this Uri.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="Uri.with"></span><span id="387" class="ts" data-target="#details-387" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">with</span>(<span class="ident">change</span>: {authority: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, fragment: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, path: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, query: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, scheme: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>}): <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span>

Derive a new Uri from this Uri.

    let file = Uri.parse('before:some/file/path');
    let other = file.with({ scheme: 'after' });
    assert.ok(other.toString() === 'after:some/file/path');

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="change"></span><span id="388" class="ts" data-target="#details-388" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">change</span><span>: </span>{authority: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, fragment: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, path: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, query: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, scheme: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>}</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>An object that describes a change to this Uri. To unset components use <code>null</code> or the empty string.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A new Uri that reflects the given change. Will return <code>this</code> Uri if the change is not changing anything.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="WorkspaceConfiguration"></span><span id="893" class="code-item">WorkspaceConfiguration</span>

Represents the configuration. It is a merged view of

- Default configuration
- Global configuration
- Workspace configuration (if available)
- Workspace folder configuration of the requested resource (if available)

_Global configuration_ comes from User Settings and shadows Defaults.

_Workspace configuration_ comes from Workspace Settings and shadows Global configuration.

_Workspace Folder configuration_ comes from `.vscode` folder under one of the [workspace folders](#workspace.workspaceFolders).

_Note:_ Workspace and Workspace Folder configurations contains `launch` and `tasks` settings. Their basename will be part of the section identifier. The following snippets shows how to retrieve all configurations from `launch.json`:

    // launch.json configuration
    const config = workspace.getConfiguration('launch', vscode.window.activeTextEditor.document.uri);

    // retrieve values
    const values = config.get('configurations');

Refer to [Settings](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/getstarted/settings) for more information.

#### Methods

<span id="WorkspaceConfiguration.get"></span><span id="895" class="ts" data-target="#details-895" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">get</span>&lt;T&gt;(<span class="ident">section</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

Return a value from this configuration.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="section"></span><span id="897" class="ts" data-target="#details-897" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">section</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Configuration name, supports <em>dotted</em> names.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">T</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The value <code>section</code> denotes or <code>undefined</code>.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="WorkspaceConfiguration.get"></span><span id="898" class="ts" data-target="#details-898" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">get</span>&lt;T&gt;(<span class="ident">section</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">defaultValue</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span></span>

Return a value from this configuration.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="section"></span><span id="900" class="ts" data-target="#details-900" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">section</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Configuration name, supports <em>dotted</em> names.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="defaultValue"></span><span id="901" class="ts" data-target="#details-901" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">defaultValue</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">T</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A value should be returned when no value could be found, is <code>undefined</code>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">T</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The value <code>section</code> denotes or the default.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="WorkspaceConfiguration.has"></span><span id="903" class="ts" data-target="#details-903" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">has</span>(<span class="ident">section</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span>

Check if this configuration has a certain value.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="section"></span><span id="904" class="ts" data-target="#details-904" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">section</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Configuration name, supports <em>dotted</em> names.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p><code>true</code> if the section doesn't resolve to <code>undefined</code>.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="WorkspaceConfiguration.inspect"></span><span id="906" class="ts" data-target="#details-906" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">inspect</span>&lt;T&gt;(<span class="ident">section</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>): {defaultValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>, globalValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>, key: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, workspaceFolderValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>, workspaceValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>} | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span>

Retrieve all information about a configuration setting. A configuration value often consists of a _default_ value, a global or installation-wide value, a workspace-specific value and a folder-specific value.

The _effective_ value (returned by [`get`](#WorkspaceConfiguration.get)) is computed like this: `defaultValue` overwritten by `globalValue`, `globalValue` overwritten by `workspaceValue`. `workspaceValue` overwritten by `workspaceFolderValue`. Refer to [Settings Inheritence](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/getstarted/settings) for more information.

_Note:_ The configuration name must denote a leaf in the configuration tree (`editor.fontSize` vs `editor`) otherwise no result is returned.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="section"></span><span id="908" class="ts" data-target="#details-908" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">section</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Configuration name, supports <em>dotted</em> names.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts">{defaultValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>, globalValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>, key: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, workspaceFolderValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>, workspaceValue: <span class="type-intrinsic">T</span>} | <span class="type-intrinsic">undefined</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Information about a configuration setting or <code>undefined</code>.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="WorkspaceConfiguration.update"></span><span id="916" class="ts" data-target="#details-916" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">update</span>(<span class="ident">section</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">value</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">any</span>, <span class="ident">configurationTarget</span>?: <span class="type-unknown">ConfigurationTarget.Global</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ConfigurationTarget.Workspace</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ConfigurationTarget.WorkspaceFolder</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span>): <a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">void</span>&gt;</span>

Update a configuration value. The updated configuration values are persisted.

A value can be changed in

- [Global configuration](#ConfigurationTarget.Global): Changes the value for all instances of the editor.
- [Workspace configuration](#ConfigurationTarget.Workspace): Changes the value for current workspace, if available.
- [Workspace folder configuration](#ConfigurationTarget.WorkspaceFolder): Changes the value for the [Workspace folder](#workspace.workspaceFolders) to which the current [configuration](#WorkspaceConfiguration) is scoped to.

_Note 1:_ Setting a global value in the presence of a more specific workspace value has no observable effect in that workspace, but in others. Setting a workspace value in the presence of a more specific folder value has no observable effect for the resources under respective [folder](#workspace.workspaceFolders), but in others. Refer to [Settings Inheritence](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/getstarted/settings) for more information.

_Note 2:_ To remove a configuration value use `undefined`, like so: `config.update('somekey', undefined)`

Will throw error when

- Writing a configuration which is not registered.
- Writing a configuration to workspace or folder target when no workspace is opened
- Writing a configuration to folder target when there is no folder settings
- Writing to folder target without passing a resource when getting the configuration (`workspace.getConfiguration(section, resource)`)
- Writing a window configuration to folder target

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="section"></span><span id="917" class="ts" data-target="#details-917" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">section</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>Configuration name, supports <em>dotted</em> names.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="value"></span><span id="918" class="ts" data-target="#details-918" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">value</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">any</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The new value.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span id="configurationTarget"></span><span id="919" class="ts" data-target="#details-919" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">configurationTarget</span><span>?</span><span>: </span><span class="type-unknown">ConfigurationTarget.Global</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ConfigurationTarget.Workspace</span> | <span class="type-unknown">ConfigurationTarget.WorkspaceFolder</span> | <span class="type-intrinsic">boolean</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The <a href="#ConfigurationTarget">configuration target</a> or a boolean value. If <code>undefined</code> or <code>null</code> or <code>false</code> configuration target is <code>ConfigurationTarget.Workspace</code>. If <code>true</code> configuration target is <code>ConfigurationTarget.Global</code>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="odd"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#Thenable" class="type-ref">Thenable</a>&lt;<span class="type-intrinsic">void</span>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

### <span id="WorkspaceEdit"></span><span id="659" class="code-item">WorkspaceEdit</span>

A workspace edit represents textual changes for many documents.

#### Properties

<span id="WorkspaceEdit.size"></span><span id="660" class="ts" data-target="#details-660" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">size</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

#### Methods

### <span id="WorkspaceFolder"></span><span id="1209" class="code-item">WorkspaceFolder</span>

A workspace folder is one of potentially many roots opened by the editor. All workspace folders are equal which means there is notion of an active or master workspace folder.

#### Properties

<span id="WorkspaceFolder.index"></span><span id="1212" class="ts" data-target="#details-1212" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">index</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">number</span></span>

The ordinal number of this workspace folder.

<span id="WorkspaceFolder.name"></span><span id="1211" class="ts" data-target="#details-1211" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">name</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span>

The name of this workspace folder. Defaults to the basename its [uri-path](#Uri.path)

<span id="WorkspaceFolder.uri"></span><span id="1210" class="ts" data-target="#details-1210" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">uri</span>: <a href="#Uri" class="type-ref">Uri</a></span>

The associated URI for this workspace folder.

### <span id="WorkspaceFoldersChangeEvent"></span><span id="1206" class="code-item">WorkspaceFoldersChangeEvent</span>

An event describing a change to the set of [workspace folders](#workspace.workspaceFolders).

#### Properties

<span id="WorkspaceFoldersChangeEvent.added"></span><span id="1207" class="ts" data-target="#details-1207" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">added</span>: <a href="#WorkspaceFolder" class="type-ref">WorkspaceFolder</a>\[\]</span>

Added workspace folders.

<span id="WorkspaceFoldersChangeEvent.removed"></span><span id="1208" class="ts" data-target="#details-1208" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">removed</span>: <a href="#WorkspaceFolder" class="type-ref">WorkspaceFolder</a>\[\]</span>

Removed workspace folders.

### <span id="WorkspaceSymbolProvider"></span><span id="619" class="code-item">WorkspaceSymbolProvider</span>

The workspace symbol provider interface defines the contract between extensions and the [symbol search](https://code.visualstudio.com/docs/editor/editingevolved#_open-symbol-by-name)-feature.

#### Methods

<span id="WorkspaceSymbolProvider.provideWorkspaceSymbols"></span><span id="621" class="ts" data-target="#details-621" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">provideWorkspaceSymbols</span>(<span class="ident">query</span>: <span class="type-intrinsic">string</span>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#SymbolInformation" class="type-ref">SymbolInformation</a>\[\]&gt;</span>

Project-wide search for a symbol matching the given query string. It is up to the provider how to search given the query string, like substring, indexOf etc. To improve performance implementors can skip the [location](#SymbolInformation.location) of symbols and implement `resolveWorkspaceSymbol` to do that later.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="query"></span><span id="622" class="ts" data-target="#details-622" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">query</span><span>: </span><span class="type-intrinsic">string</span></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A non-empty query string.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="623" class="ts" data-target="#details-623" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#SymbolInformation" class="type-ref">SymbolInformation</a>[]&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>An array of document highlights or a thenable that resolves to such. The lack of a result can be signaled by returning <code>undefined</code>, <code>null</code>, or an empty array.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>

<span id="WorkspaceSymbolProvider.resolveWorkspaceSymbol"></span><span id="625" class="ts" data-target="#details-625" toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">resolveWorkspaceSymbol</span>(<span class="ident">symbol</span>: <a href="#SymbolInformation" class="type-ref">SymbolInformation</a>, <span class="ident">token</span>: <a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a>): <a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#SymbolInformation" class="type-ref">SymbolInformation</a>&gt;</span>

Given a symbol fill in its [location](#SymbolInformation.location). This method is called whenever a symbol is selected in the UI. Providers can implement this method and return incomplete symbols from [`provideWorkspaceSymbols`](#WorkspaceSymbolProvider.provideWorkspaceSymbols) which often helps to improve performance.

<table class="table table-bordered"><colgroup><col style="width: 50%" /><col style="width: 50%" /></colgroup><thead><tr class="header"><th>Parameter</th><th>Description</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr class="odd"><th><span id="symbol"></span><span id="626" class="ts" data-target="#details-626" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">symbol</span><span>: </span><a href="#SymbolInformation" class="type-ref">SymbolInformation</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The symbol that is to be resolved. Guaranteed to be an instance of an object returned from an earlier call to <code>provideWorkspaceSymbols</code>.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span id="token"></span><span id="627" class="ts" data-target="#details-627" data-toggle="collapse"><span class="ident">token</span><span>: </span><a href="#CancellationToken" class="type-ref">CancellationToken</a></span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>A cancellation token.</p></div></th></tr><tr class="odd"><th>Returns</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr class="even"><th><span class="ts"><a href="#ProviderResult" class="type-ref">ProviderResult</a>&lt;<a href="#SymbolInformation" class="type-ref">SymbolInformation</a>&gt;</span></th><th><div class="comment"><p>The resolved symbol or a thenable that resolves to that. When no result is returned, the given <code>symbol</code> is used.</p></div></th></tr></tbody></table>
